Student* Task6_09::pop() {
    if (first) {
        Node *current = first, *new_last = nullptr;
        // –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±–æ—Ä —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –≤ new_last –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏–π —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç
        while (current->next) {
            new_last = current;
            current = current->next;
        }

        Student* st = new Student(last->item);
        // new_last –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç—å—Å—è nullptr –µ—Å–ª–∏ –µ—Å—Ç—å –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –æ–¥–∏–Ω —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤ —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫–µ
        if (new_last) new_last->next = nullptr;
        delete last;
        last = new_last;
        return st;
    } else
        return nullptr;
}

void Cursework::encrypt (std::string filenameIn, std::string filenameOut, std::string key) {
    std::string command = "openssl aes-128-cbc -salt -in " + filenameIn + " -out " + filenameOut + " -pass pass:" + key;
    std::system(command.c_str());
    if (std::remove(filenameIn.c_str()) != 0) {
        std::cerr << "CANNOT DELETE >>> " + filenameIn << std::endl;
    }
}

In reply to this message 
short Database::Encrypt(string filein, string fileout, string pass) {
    if (!prepareSSL()) {
       return 1;
    }

    if (!pass.length()) pass = generatePassword();
    ofstream writekey("key.txt");
    writekey << pass;
    writekey.close();
    system("openssl\\bin\\openssl.exe pkeyutl -encrypt -inkey rsa.public -pubin -in key.txt -out key.txt.enc");

    string cmd = "openssl\\bin\\openssl.exe enc -aes-256-cbc -salt -in " + filein  + " -out " +  fileout + " -pass file:key.txt";
    system(cmd.c_str());

    remove("key.txt");
    remove(filein.c_str());
    return 0;
}

enum Gender {
    Male,
    Female
};

struct EducationData {
    wstring institute;
    wstring kafedra;
    wstring group;
};

struct ExamData {
    short semester;
    wstring subject;
    short mark;
};

struct Student {
    wstring id;
    wstring last_name;
    wstring first_name;
    wstring father_name;
    wstring date_of_birth;
    int entered_year;
    EducationData education_data;
    Gender gender;
    vector<ExamData> exam_marks;
};

class Database
{
    // –ö–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
    vector<Student> data;
    bool block_output = false;
    bool less_text = true;

    // –í—Å–ø–æ–º–æ–≥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏
    Student* find(Student);
    bool prepareSSL();
    string generatePassword();
public:
    ConsoleTools console;

    Database();
    Database(vector<Student>);
    void setsettings();
    short readFromFile(string);
    short writeToFile(string);

    void addLine(bool, size_t index);
    void updateLine(size_t index);
    Student* deleteLine(size_t index);
    void clear();
    void solve();

    short Encrypt(string, string="", string="");
    short Decrypt(string, string="", string="");

    friend wostream& operator <<(wostream&, Database);
};

#endif // DATABASE_H

struct grade {
    std::string subject;
    std::string date;
    short mark;
};


struct student {
    std::string number;
    std::string first_name;
    std::string middle_name;
    std::string last_name;
    unsigned short year;
    std::string birthday;
    std::string faculty;
    std::string department;
    std::string group;
    std::string gender;
    grade result;
    bool operator== (student& unit) const;
};


class Cursework {
private:
    List <student> database;
public:
    Cursework ();
    Cursework (const Cursework& unit);
    Cursework (const std::string filename);
    Cursework& operator= (const Cursework& unit);
    friend std::ostream& operator<< (std::ostream& os, Cursework& unit);
    ~Cursework ();
    void append (const student unit);
    void remove (const unsigned int index);
    std::pair <List <student>, List <student>> split (std::string group);
    List <student> findBadStudents ();
    List <student> findGoodStudents ();
    static void encrypt (std::string filenameIn, std::string filenameOut, std::string key);
    static void decrypt (std::string filenameIn, std::string filenameOut, std::string key);
};

#define DATAENTITY_H

#include <fstream>
#include <string>
#include <regex>

enum Value_type {
    NO_VALIDATE,
    STRING_LIKE,
    NUMBER_LIKE
};

template<typename T>
class DataEntity
{
private:
    std::wstring name;
    std::wstring color;
    short space_required;
    std::wstring pattern;
    Value_type value_type;

    T value;
public:
    DataEntity(std::wstring, std::wstring, short, std::wstring = L"", Value_type = NO_VALIDATE);

    bool validate(T);
    T get() {return value;};
    bool set(T);

    friend std::wostream& operator <<(std::wostream&, T);
};

#endif // DATAENTITY_H
